## Diagram 2

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
    [*] --> CheckCreate
    CheckCreate --> GenerateMetadata: create=true
    CheckCreate --> [*]: create=false
    GenerateMetadata --> SetName
    SetName --> SetNamespace
    SetNamespace --> ApplyLabels
    ApplyLabels --> CheckAnnotations
    CheckAnnotations --> ApplyAnnotations: annotations exist
    CheckAnnotations --> Complete: no annotations
    ApplyAnnotations --> Complete
    Complete --> [*]
```
